Submission Title	Transcription profiling of mouse samples - re-analysis of data on the MG_U74Av2 platform
Submission Identifier	GAE-MTAB-27
Submission Description	This is a dataset of integrated high quality mouse expression data generated on affymetrix MG_U74Av2 platform. The original data were selected from ArrayExpress. Please refer to the original ArrayExpress experiments to find additional details. The normalized data file is updated on 2009-07-17.
